with both municipalities for Class III Officers.  The below three areas wer=
e fixed in the attached draft.  As you can see minor clarifications.

Pages 3-4

d "can" or "may"?  May was identified and the word "can" was deleted.

Page 6

Page 7-8

Section VIII(I) - is blank. (This blank was removed)

I have attached the updated drafts.

Thanks for all your support.
